:orphan:

.. _named-color-list:

Named colors
############

The current list of named colors stems from Matplotlib's :code:`colors` module, specifically the global variables :code:`BASE_COLORS`, :code:`CSS4_COLORS`, :code:`TABLEAU_COLORS` and :code:`XKCD_COLORS`. These names are made available both for Matplotlib and Plotly figures.

-----------
